posted:Posted November 20, 2023
msg:I don't know how they got such good reviews, because I like to go out and travel frequently, and it has been a long time since a hotel made me feel this way!
First, you can't use the ID card photo authenticated by Alipay when checking in, you must have the original one, if this is a national rule, ok.
Second, you have to pay a deposit of 300 first, and when you pay, they say you will be back in ten minutes after checkout, and when I check out, they say before 3 pm? ? Not to mention how many 4.5-star hotels I have stayed in over the years that don't require a deposit, there is no conclusion on how long it will take to return.
Third, takeaways are not allowed to be delivered to the floor, and the waiter doesn't deliver them either, and I have to come down to get them? ? ? Is this a 5-star service standard? ?
Fourth, the breakfast is very ordinary, and it is completely incomparable with the five-star R&F Wanda.
Fifth, the TV remote control must first press the right power button to turn off the TV, then press the left to open the box, and then press the right to turn on the TV... I have to study the TV for a long time, it's really drunk...
Sixth, the environment is very ordinary, not as good as Vienna, how did this five-star hotel come from?
After staying in so many four- and five-star hotels, this one is the one that makes me want to criticize it the most.
